    23	var logKind = logf.RuntimeLog.WithName("source").WithName("Kind")
    24	
    25	// Kind is used to provide a source of events originating inside the cluster from Watches (e.g. Pod Create).
    26	type Kind[object client.Object, request comparable] struct {
    27	        // Type is the type of object to watch.  e.g. &v1.Pod{}
    28	        Type object
    29	
    30	        // Cache used to watch APIs
    31	        Cache cache.Cache
    32	
    33	        Handler handler.TypedEventHandler[object, request]
    34	
    35	        Predicates []predicate.TypedPredicate[object]
    36	
    37	        // startedErr may contain an error if one was encountered during startup. If its closed and does not
    38	        // contain an error, startup and syncing finished.
    39	        startedErr  chan error
    40	        startCancel func()
    41	}
    42	
    43	// Start is internal and should be called only by the Controller to register an EventHandler with the Informer
    44	// to enqueue reconcile.Requests.
    45	func (ks *Kind[object, request]) Start(ctx context.Context, queue workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[request]) error {
    46	        if isNil(ks.Type) {
    47	                return fmt.Errorf("must create Kind with a non-nil object")
    48	        }
    49	        if isNil(ks.Cache) {
    50	                return fmt.Errorf("must create Kind with a non-nil cache")
    51	        }
    52	        if isNil(ks.Handler) {
    53	                return errors.New("must create Kind with non-nil handler")
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        // cache.GetInformer will block until its context is cancelled if the cache was already started and it can not
    57	        // sync that informer (most commonly due to RBAC issues).
    58	        ctx, ks.startCancel = context.WithCancel(ctx)
    59	        ks.startedErr = make(chan error, 1) // Buffer chan to not leak goroutines if WaitForSync isn't called
    60	        go func() {
    61	                var (
    62	                        i       cache.Informer
    63	                        lastErr error
    64	                )
    65	
    66	                // Tries to get an informer until it returns true,
    67	                // an error or the specified context is cancelled or expired.
    68	                if err := wait.PollUntilContextCancel(ctx, 10*time.Second, true, func(ctx context.Context) (bool, error) {
    69	                        // Lookup the Informer from the Cache and add an EventHandler which populates the Queue
    70	                        i, lastErr = ks.Cache.GetInformer(ctx, ks.Type)
    71	                        if lastErr != nil {
    72	                                kindMatchErr := &meta.NoKindMatchError{}
    73	                                switch {
    74	                                case errors.As(lastErr, &kindMatchErr):
    75	                                        logKind.Error(lastErr, "if kind is a CRD, it should be installed before calling Start",
    76	                                                "kind", kindMatchErr.GroupKind)
    77	                                case runtime.IsNotRegisteredError(lastErr):
    78	                                        logKind.Error(lastErr, "kind must be registered to the Scheme")
    79	                                default:
    80	                                        logKind.Error(lastErr, "failed to get informer from cache")
    81	                                }
    82	                                return false, nil // Retry.
    83	                        }
    84	                        return true, nil
    85	                }); err != nil {
    86	                        if lastErr != nil {
    87	                                ks.startedErr <- fmt.Errorf("failed to get informer from cache: %w", lastErr)
    88	                                return
    89	                        }
    90	                        ks.startedErr <- err
    91	                        return
    92	                }
    93	
    94	                handlerRegistration, err := i.AddEventHandlerWithOptions(NewEventHandler(ctx, queue, ks.Handler, ks.Predicates), toolscache.HandlerOptions{
    95	                        Logger: &logKind,
    96	                })
    97	                if err != nil {
    98	                        ks.startedErr <- err
    99	                        return
   100	                }
   101	                // First, wait for the cache to sync. For real caches this waits for startup.
   102	                // For fakes with Synced=false, this returns immediately allowing fast failure.
   103	                if !ks.Cache.WaitForCacheSync(ctx) {
   104	                        ks.startedErr <- errors.New("cache did not sync")
   105	                        close(ks.startedErr)
   106	                        return
   107	                }
   108	                // Then wait for this specific handler to receive all initial events.
   109	                if !toolscache.WaitForCacheSync(ctx.Done(), handlerRegistration.HasSynced) {
   110	                        ks.startedErr <- errors.New("handler did not sync")
   111	                }
   112	                close(ks.startedErr)
   113	        }()
   114	
   115	        return nil
   116	}
   117	
   118	func (ks *Kind[object, request]) String() string {
   119	        if !isNil(ks.Type) {
   120	                return fmt.Sprintf("kind source: %T", ks.Type)
   121	        }
   122	        return "kind source: unknown type"
   123	}
   124	
   125	// WaitForSync implements SyncingSource to allow controllers to wait with starting
   126	// workers until the cache is synced.
   127	func (ks *Kind[object, request]) WaitForSync(ctx context.Context) error {
   128	        select {
   129	        case err := <-ks.startedErr:
   130	                return err
   131	        case <-ctx.Done():
   132	                ks.startCancel()
   133	                if errors.Is(ctx.Err(), context.Canceled) {
   134	                        return nil
   135	                }
   136	                return fmt.Errorf("timed out waiting for cache to be synced for Kind %T", ks.Type)
   137	        }
   138	}
   139	
   140	func isNil(arg any) bool {
   141	        if v := reflect.ValueOf(arg); !v.IsValid() || ((v.Kind() == reflect.Ptr ||
   142	                v.Kind() == reflect.Interface ||
   143	                v.Kind() == reflect.Slice ||
   144	                v.Kind() == reflect.Map ||
   145	                v.Kind() == reflect.Chan ||
   146	                v.Kind() == reflect.Func) && v.IsNil()) {
   147	                return true
   148	        }
   149	        return false
   150	}

   160	        object client.Object,
   161	        eventHandler handler.TypedEventHandler[client.Object, request],
   162	        opts ...WatchesOption,
   163	) *TypedBuilder[request] {
   164	        input := WatchesInput[request]{
   165	                obj:     object,
   166	                handler: eventHandler,
   167	        }
   168	        for _, opt := range opts {
   169	                opt.ApplyToWatches(&input)
   170	        }
   171	
   172	        blder.watchesInput = append(blder.watchesInput, input)
   173	
   174	        return blder
   175	}
   176	
   177	// WatchesMetadata is the same as Watches, but forces the internal cache to only watch PartialObjectMetadata.
   178	//
   179	// This is useful when watching lots of objects, really big objects, or objects for which you only know
   180	// the GVK, but not the structure. You'll need to pass metav1.PartialObjectMetadata to the client
   181	// when fetching objects in your reconciler, otherwise you'll end up with a duplicate structured or unstructured cache.
   182	//
   183	// When watching a resource with metadata only, for example the v1.Pod, you should not Get and List using the v1.Pod type.
   184	// Instead, you should use the special metav1.PartialObjectMetadata type.
   185	//
   186	// ❌ Incorrect:
   187	//
   188	//      pod := &v1.Pod{}
   189	//      mgr.GetClient().Get(ctx, nsAndName, pod)
   190	//
   191	// ✅ Correct:
   192	//
   193	//      pod := &metav1.PartialObjectMetadata{}
   194	//      pod.SetGroupVersionKind(schema.GroupVersionKind{
   195	//          Group:   "",
   196	//          Version: "v1",
   197	//          Kind:    "Pod",
   198	//      })
   199	//      mgr.GetClient().Get(ctx, nsAndName, pod)
   200	//
   201	// In the first case, controller-runtime will create another cache for the
   202	// concrete type on top of the metadata cache; this increases memory
   203	// consumption and leads to race conditions as caches are not in sync.
   204	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) WatchesMetadata(
   205	        object client.Object,
   206	        eventHandler handler.TypedEventHandler[client.Object, request],
   207	        opts ...WatchesOption,
   208	) *TypedBuilder[request] {
   209	        opts = append(opts, OnlyMetadata)
   210	        return blder.Watches(object, eventHandler, opts...)
   211	}
   212	
   213	// WatchesRawSource exposes the lower-level ControllerManagedBy Watches functions through the builder.
   214	//
   215	// WatchesRawSource does not respect predicates configured through WithEventFilter.
   216	//
   217	// WatchesRawSource makes it possible to use typed handlers and predicates with `source.Kind` as well as custom source implementations.
   218	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) WatchesRawSource(src source.TypedSource[request]) *TypedBuilder[request] {
   219	        blder.rawSources = append(blder.rawSources, src)
   220	
   221	        return blder
   222	}
   223	
   224	// WithEventFilter sets the event filters, to filter which create/update/delete/generic events eventually
   225	// trigger reconciliations. For example, filtering on whether the resource version has changed.
   226	// Given predicate is added for all watched objects and thus must be able to deal with the type
   227	// of all watched objects.
   228	//
   229	// Defaults to the empty list.
   230	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) WithEventFilter(p predicate.Predicate) *TypedBuilder[request] {
   231	        blder.globalPredicates = append(blder.globalPredicates, p)
   232	        return blder
   233	}
   234	
   235	// WithOptions overrides the controller options used in doController. Defaults to empty.
   236	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) WithOptions(options controller.TypedOptions[request]) *TypedBuilder[request] {
   237	        blder.ctrlOptions = options
   238	        return blder
   239	}
   240	
   241	// WithLogConstructor overrides the controller options's LogConstructor.
   242	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) WithLogConstructor(logConstructor func(*request) logr.Logger) *TypedBuilder[request] {
   243	        blder.ctrlOptions.LogConstructor = logConstructor
   244	        return blder
   245	}
   246	
   247	// Named sets the name of the controller to the given name. The name shows up
   248	// in metrics, among other things, and thus should be a prometheus compatible name
   249	// (underscores and alphanumeric characters only).
   250	//
   251	// By default, controllers are named using the lowercase version of their kind.
   252	//
   253	// The name must be unique as it is used to identify the controller in metrics and logs.
   254	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) Named(name string) *TypedBuilder[request] {
   255	        blder.name = name
   256	        return blder
   257	}
   258	
   259	// Complete builds the Application Controller.
   260	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) Complete(r reconcile.TypedReconciler[request]) error {
   261	        _, err := blder.Build(r)
   262	        return err
   263	}
   264	
   265	// Build builds the Application Controller and returns the Controller it created.
   266	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) Build(r reconcile.TypedReconciler[request]) (controller.TypedController[request], error) {
   267	        if r == nil {
   268	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("must provide a non-nil Reconciler")
   269	        }
   270	        if blder.mgr == nil {
   271	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("must provide a non-nil Manager")
   272	        }
   273	        if blder.forInput.err != nil {
   274	                return nil, blder.forInput.err
   275	        }
   276	
   277	        // Set the ControllerManagedBy
   278	        if err := blder.doController(r); err != nil {
   279	                return nil, err
   280	        }
   281	
   282	        // Set the Watch
   283	        if err := blder.doWatch(); err != nil {
   284	                return nil, err
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        return blder.ctrl, nil
   288	}
   289	
   290	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) project(obj client.Object, proj objectProjection) (client.Object, error) {
   291	        switch proj {
   292	        case projectAsNormal:
   293	                return obj, nil
   294	        case projectAsMetadata:
   295	                metaObj := &metav1.PartialObjectMetadata{}
   296	                gvk, err := apiutil.GVKForObject(obj, blder.mgr.GetScheme())
   297	                if err != nil {
   298	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to determine GVK of %T for a metadata-only watch: %w", obj, err)
   299	                }
   300	                metaObj.SetGroupVersionKind(gvk)
   301	                return metaObj, nil
   302	        default:
   303	                panic(fmt.Sprintf("unexpected projection type %v on type %T, should not be possible since this is an internal field", proj, obj))
   304	        }
   305	}
   306	
   307	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) doWatch() error {
   308	        // Reconcile type
   309	        if blder.forInput.object != nil {
   310	                obj, err := blder.project(blder.forInput.object, blder.forInput.objectProjection)
   311	                if err != nil {
   312	                        return err
   313	                }
   314	
   315	                if reflect.TypeFor[request]() != reflect.TypeFor[reconcile.Request]() {
   316	                        return fmt.Errorf("For() can only be used with reconcile.Request, got %T", *new(request))
   317	                }
   318	
   319	                var hdler handler.TypedEventHandler[client.Object, request]
   320	                reflect.ValueOf(&hdler).Elem().Set(reflect.ValueOf(&handler.EnqueueRequestForObject{}))
   321	                allPredicates := append([]predicate.Predicate(nil), blder.globalPredicates...)
   322	                allPredicates = append(allPredicates, blder.forInput.predicates...)
   323	                src := source.TypedKind(blder.mgr.GetCache(), obj, hdler, allPredicates...)
   324	                if err := blder.ctrl.Watch(src); err != nil {
   325	                        return err

   380	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) getControllerName(gvk schema.GroupVersionKind, hasGVK bool) (string, error) {
   381	        if blder.name != "" {
   382	                return blder.name, nil
   383	        }
   384	        if !hasGVK {
   385	                return "", errors.New("one of For() or Named() must be called")
   386	        }
   387	        return strings.ToLower(gvk.Kind), nil
   388	}
   389	
   390	func (blder *TypedBuilder[request]) doController(r reconcile.TypedReconciler[request]) error {
   391	        globalOpts := blder.mgr.GetControllerOptions()
   392	
   393	        ctrlOptions := blder.ctrlOptions
   394	        if ctrlOptions.Reconciler != nil && r != nil {
   395	                return errors.New("reconciler was set via WithOptions() and via Build() or Complete()")
   396	        }
   397	        if ctrlOptions.Reconciler == nil {
   398	                ctrlOptions.Reconciler = r
   399	        }
   400	
   401	        // Retrieve the GVK from the object we're reconciling
   402	        // to pre-populate logger information, and to optionally generate a default name.
   403	        var gvk schema.GroupVersionKind
   404	        hasGVK := blder.forInput.object != nil
   405	        if hasGVK {
   406	                var err error
   407	                gvk, err = apiutil.GVKForObject(blder.forInput.object, blder.mgr.GetScheme())
   408	                if err != nil {
   409	                        return err
   410	                }
   411	        }
   412	
   413	        // Setup concurrency.
   414	        if ctrlOptions.MaxConcurrentReconciles == 0 && hasGVK {
   415	                groupKind := gvk.GroupKind().String()
   416	
   417	                if concurrency, ok := globalOpts.GroupKindConcurrency[groupKind]; ok && concurrency > 0 {
   418	                        ctrlOptions.MaxConcurrentReconciles = concurrency
   419	                }
   420	        }
   421	
   422	        // Setup cache sync timeout.
   423	        if ctrlOptions.CacheSyncTimeout == 0 && globalOpts.CacheSyncTimeout > 0 {
   424	                ctrlOptions.CacheSyncTimeout = globalOpts.CacheSyncTimeout
   425	        }
   426	
   427	        controllerName, err := blder.getControllerName(gvk, hasGVK)
   428	        if err != nil {
   429	                return err
   430	        }

    38	var logInformer = logf.RuntimeLog.WithName("source").WithName("Informer")
    39	
    40	// Source is a source of events (e.g. Create, Update, Delete operations on Kubernetes Objects, Webhook callbacks, etc)
    41	// which should be processed by event.EventHandlers to enqueue reconcile.Requests.
    42	//
    43	// * Use Kind for events originating in the cluster (e.g. Pod Create, Pod Update, Deployment Update).
    44	//
    45	// * Use Channel for events originating outside the cluster (e.g. GitHub Webhook callback, Polling external urls).
    46	//
    47	// Users may build their own Source implementations.
    48	type Source = TypedSource[reconcile.Request]
    49	
    50	// TypedSource is a generic source of events (e.g. Create, Update, Delete operations on Kubernetes Objects, Webhook callbacks, etc)
    51	// which should be processed by event.EventHandlers to enqueue a request.
    52	//
    53	// * Use Kind for events originating in the cluster (e.g. Pod Create, Pod Update, Deployment Update).
    54	//
    55	// * Use Channel for events originating outside the cluster (e.g. GitHub Webhook callback, Polling external urls).
    56	//
    57	// Users may build their own Source implementations.
    58	type TypedSource[request comparable] interface {
    59	        // Start is internal and should be called only by the Controller to start the source.
    60	        // Start must be non-blocking.
    61	        Start(context.Context, workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[request]) error
    62	}
    63	
    64	// SyncingSource is a source that needs syncing prior to being usable. The controller
    65	// will call its WaitForSync prior to starting workers.
    66	type SyncingSource = TypedSyncingSource[reconcile.Request]
    67	
    68	// TypedSyncingSource is a source that needs syncing prior to being usable. The controller
    69	// will call its WaitForSync prior to starting workers.
    70	type TypedSyncingSource[request comparable] interface {
    71	        TypedSource[request]
    72	        WaitForSync(ctx context.Context) error
    73	}
    74	
    75	// Kind creates a KindSource with the given cache provider.
    76	func Kind[object client.Object](
    77	        cache cache.Cache,
    78	        obj object,
    79	        handler handler.TypedEventHandler[object, reconcile.Request],
    80	        predicates ...predicate.TypedPredicate[object],
    81	) SyncingSource {
    82	        return TypedKind(cache, obj, handler, predicates...)
    83	}
    84	
    85	// TypedKind creates a KindSource with the given cache provider.
    86	func TypedKind[object client.Object, request comparable](
    87	        cache cache.Cache,
    88	        obj object,
    89	        handler handler.TypedEventHandler[object, request],
    90	        predicates ...predicate.TypedPredicate[object],
    91	) TypedSyncingSource[request] {
    92	        return &internal.Kind[object, request]{
    93	                Type:       obj,
    94	                Cache:      cache,
    95	                Handler:    handler,
    96	                Predicates: predicates,
    97	        }
    98	}
    99	
   100	var _ Source = &channel[string, reconcile.Request]{}
   101	
   102	// ChannelOpt allows to configure a source.Channel.
   103	type ChannelOpt[object any, request comparable] func(*channel[object, request])
   104	
   105	// WithPredicates adds the configured predicates to a source.Channel.
   106	func WithPredicates[object any, request comparable](p ...predicate.TypedPredicate[object]) ChannelOpt[object, request] {
   107	        return func(c *channel[object, request]) {
   108	                c.predicates = append(c.predicates, p...)
   109	        }
   110	}
   111	
   112	// WithBufferSize configures the buffer size for a source.Channel. By
   113	// default, the buffer size is 1024.
   114	func WithBufferSize[object any, request comparable](bufferSize int) ChannelOpt[object, request] {
   115	        return func(c *channel[object, request]) {
   116	                c.bufferSize = &bufferSize
   117	        }
   118	}
   119	
   120	// Channel is used to provide a source of events originating outside the cluster
   121	// (e.g. GitHub Webhook callback).  Channel requires the user to wire the external
   122	// source (e.g. http handler) to write GenericEvents to the underlying channel.
   123	func Channel[object any](
   124	        source <-chan event.TypedGenericEvent[object],
   125	        handler handler.TypedEventHandler[object, reconcile.Request],
   126	        opts ...ChannelOpt[object, reconcile.Request],
   127	) Source {
   128	        return TypedChannel[object, reconcile.Request](source, handler, opts...)
   129	}
   130	
   131	// TypedChannel is used to provide a source of events originating outside the cluster
   132	// (e.g. GitHub Webhook callback).  Channel requires the user to wire the external
   133	// source (e.g. http handler) to write GenericEvents to the underlying channel.
   134	func TypedChannel[object any, request comparable](
   135	        source <-chan event.TypedGenericEvent[object],
   136	        handler handler.TypedEventHandler[object, request],
   137	        opts ...ChannelOpt[object, request],
   138	) TypedSource[request] {
   139	        c := &channel[object, request]{
   140	                source:  source,
   141	                handler: handler,
   142	        }
   143	        for _, opt := range opts {
   144	                opt(c)
   145	        }
   146	
   147	        return c
   148	}
   149	
   150	type channel[object any, request comparable] struct {

   339	// Remove removes an informer entry and stops it if it was running.
   340	func (ip *Informers) Remove(gvk schema.GroupVersionKind, obj runtime.Object) {
   341	        ip.mu.Lock()
   342	        defer ip.mu.Unlock()
   343	
   344	        informerMap := ip.informersByType(obj)
   345	
   346	        entry, ok := informerMap[gvk]
   347	        if !ok {
   348	                return
   349	        }
   350	        close(entry.stop)
   351	        delete(informerMap, gvk)
   352	}
   353	
   354	func (ip *Informers) informersByType(obj runtime.Object) map[schema.GroupVersionKind]*Cache {
   355	        switch obj.(type) {
   356	        case runtime.Unstructured:
   357	                return ip.tracker.Unstructured
   358	        case *metav1.PartialObjectMetadata, *metav1.PartialObjectMetadataList:
   359	                return ip.tracker.Metadata
   360	        default:
   361	                return ip.tracker.Structured
   362	        }
   363	}
   364	
   365	// addInformerToMap either returns an existing informer or creates a new informer, adds it to the map and returns it.
   366	func (ip *Informers) addInformerToMap(gvk schema.GroupVersionKind, obj runtime.Object) (*Cache, bool, error) {
   367	        ip.mu.Lock()
   368	        defer ip.mu.Unlock()
   369	
   370	        // Check the cache to see if we already have an Informer. If we do, return the Informer.
   371	        // This is for the case where 2 routines tried to get the informer when it wasn't in the map
   372	        // so neither returned early, but the first one created it.
   373	        if i, ok := ip.informersByType(obj)[gvk]; ok {
   374	                return i, ip.started, nil
   375	        }
   376	
   377	        // Create a NewSharedIndexInformer and add it to the map.
   378	        listWatcher, err := ip.makeListWatcher(gvk, obj)
   379	        if err != nil {
   380	                return nil, false, err
   381	        }
   382	        sharedIndexInformer := ip.newInformer(&cache.ListWatch{
   383	                ListWithContextFunc: func(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (runtime.Object, error) {
   384	                        ip.selector.ApplyToList(&opts)
   385	                        return listWatcher.ListWithContextFunc(ctx, opts)
   386	                },
   387	                WatchFuncWithContext: func(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (watch.Interface, error) {
   388	                        opts.Watch = true // Watch needs to be set to true separately
   389	                        opts.AllowWatchBookmarks = ip.enableWatchBookmarks
   390	
   391	                        ip.selector.ApplyToList(&opts)
   392	                        return listWatcher.WatchFuncWithContext(ctx, opts)
   393	                },
   394	        }, obj, calculateResyncPeriod(ip.resync), cache.Indexers{
   395	                cache.NamespaceIndex: cache.MetaNamespaceIndexFunc,
   396	        })
   397	
   398	        // Set WatchErrorHandler on SharedIndexInformer if set
   399	        if ip.watchErrorHandler != nil {
   400	                if err := sharedIndexInformer.SetWatchErrorHandlerWithContext(ip.watchErrorHandler); err != nil {
   401	                        return nil, false, err
   402	                }
   403	        }
   404	
   405	        // Check to see if there is a transformer for this gvk
   406	        if err := sharedIndexInformer.SetTransform(ip.transform); err != nil {
   407	                return nil, false, err
   408	        }
   409	
   410	        mapping, err := ip.mapper.RESTMapping(gvk.GroupKind(), gvk.Version)
   411	        if err != nil {
   412	                return nil, false, err
   413	        }
   414	
   415	        // Create the new entry and set it in the map.
   416	        i := &Cache{
   417	                Informer: sharedIndexInformer,
   418	                Reader: CacheReader{
   419	                        indexer:          sharedIndexInformer.GetIndexer(),
   420	                        groupVersionKind: gvk,
   421	                        scopeName:        mapping.Scope.Name(),
   422	                        disableDeepCopy:  ip.unsafeDisableDeepCopy,
   423	                },
   424	                stop: make(chan struct{}),
   425	        }
   426	        ip.informersByType(obj)[gvk] = i
   427	
   428	        // Start the informer in case the InformersMap has started, otherwise it will be
   429	        // started when the InformersMap starts.
   430	        if ip.started {
   431	                ip.startInformerLocked(i)
   432	        }
   433	        return i, ip.started, nil
   434	}
   435	
   436	func (ip *Informers) makeListWatcher(gvk schema.GroupVersionKind, obj runtime.Object) (*cache.ListWatch, error) {
   437	        // Kubernetes APIs work against Resources, not GroupVersionKinds.  Map the
   438	        // groupVersionKind to the Resource API we will use.
   439	        mapping, err := ip.mapper.RESTMapping(gvk.GroupKind(), gvk.Version)
   440	        if err != nil {
   441	                return nil, err
   442	        }
   443	
   444	        // Figure out if the GVK we're dealing with is global, or namespace scoped.
   445	        var namespace string
   446	        if mapping.Scope.Name() == meta.RESTScopeNameNamespace {
   447	                namespace = restrictNamespaceBySelector(ip.namespace, ip.selector)
   448	        }
   449	
   450	        switch obj.(type) {
   451	        //
   452	        // Unstructured
   453	        //
   454	        case runtime.Unstructured:
   455	                // If the rest configuration has a negotiated serializer passed in,
   456	                // we should remove it and use the one that the dynamic client sets for us.
   457	                cfg := rest.CopyConfig(ip.config)
   458	                cfg.NegotiatedSerializer = nil
   459	                dynamicClient, err := dynamic.NewForConfigAndClient(cfg, ip.httpClient)
   460	                if err != nil {
   461	                        return nil, err
   462	                }
   463	                resources := dynamicClient.Resource(mapping.Resource)
   464	                return &cache.ListWatch{
   465	                        ListWithContextFunc: func(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (runtime.Object, error) {
   466	                                if namespace != "" {
   467	                                        return resources.Namespace(namespace).List(ctx, opts)
   468	                                }
   469	                                return resources.List(ctx, opts)
   470	                        },
   471	                        // Setup the watch function
   472	                        WatchFuncWithContext: func(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (watch.Interface, error) {
   473	                                opts.Watch = true // Watch needs to be set to true separately
   474	                                opts.AllowWatchBookmarks = ip.enableWatchBookmarks
   475	
   476	                                if namespace != "" {
   477	                                        return resources.Namespace(namespace).Watch(ctx, opts)
   478	                                }
   479	                                return resources.Watch(ctx, opts)
   480	                        },
   481	                }, nil
   482	        //
   483	        // Metadata
   484	        //
   485	        case *metav1.PartialObjectMetadata, *metav1.PartialObjectMetadataList:
   486	                // Always clear the negotiated serializer and use the one
   487	                // set from the metadata client.
   488	                cfg := rest.CopyConfig(ip.config)
   489	                cfg.NegotiatedSerializer = nil
   490	
   491	                // Grab the metadata metadataClient.
   492	                metadataClient, err := metadata.NewForConfigAndClient(cfg, ip.httpClient)
   493	                if err != nil {
   494	                        return nil, err
   495	                }
   496	                resources := metadataClient.Resource(mapping.Resource)
   497	
   498	                return &cache.ListWatch{
   499	                        ListWithContextFunc: func(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (runtime.Object, error) {
   500	                                var (
   501	                                        list *metav1.PartialObjectMetadataList
   502	                                        err  error
   503	                                )
   504	                                if namespace != "" {
   505	                                        list, err = resources.Namespace(namespace).List(ctx, opts)
   506	                                } else {
   507	                                        list, err = resources.List(ctx, opts)
   508	                                }
   509	                                if list != nil {
   510	                                        for i := range list.Items {
   511	                                                list.Items[i].SetGroupVersionKind(gvk)
   512	                                        }
   513	                                }
   514	                                return list, err
   515	                        },
   516	                        // Setup the watch function
   517	                        WatchFuncWithContext: func(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (watcher watch.Interface, err error) {
   518	                                opts.Watch = true // Watch needs to be set to true separately
   519	                                opts.AllowWatchBookmarks = ip.enableWatchBookmarks
   520	
   521	                                if namespace != "" {
   522	                                        watcher, err = resources.Namespace(namespace).Watch(ctx, opts)
   523	                                } else {
   524	                                        watcher, err = resources.Watch(ctx, opts)
   525	                                }
   526	                                if err != nil {
   527	                                        return nil, err
   528	                                }
   529	                                return newGVKFixupWatcher(gvk, watcher), nil
   530	                        },
   531	                }, nil
   532	        //
   533	        // Structured.
   534	        //
   535	        default:
   536	                client, err := apiutil.RESTClientForGVK(gvk, false, false, ip.config, ip.codecs, ip.httpClient)
   537	                if err != nil {
   538	                        return nil, err
   539	                }
   540	                listGVK := gvk.GroupVersion().WithKind(gvk.Kind + "List")

    48	// ErrResourceNotCached indicates that the resource type
    49	// the client asked the cache for is not cached, i.e. the
    50	// corresponding informer does not exist yet.
    51	type ErrResourceNotCached struct {
    52	        GVK schema.GroupVersionKind
    53	}
    54	
    55	// Error returns the error
    56	func (r ErrResourceNotCached) Error() string {
    57	        return fmt.Sprintf("%s is not cached", r.GVK.String())
    58	}
    59	
    60	var _ error = (*ErrResourceNotCached)(nil)

    62	// InformersOpts configures an InformerMap.
    63	type InformersOpts struct {
    64	        HTTPClient            *http.Client
    65	        Scheme                *runtime.Scheme
    66	        Mapper                meta.RESTMapper
    67	        ResyncPeriod          time.Duration
    68	        Namespace             string
    69	        NewInformer           func(cache.ListerWatcher, runtime.Object, time.Duration, cache.Indexers) cache.SharedIndexInformer
    70	        Selector              Selector
    71	        Transform             cache.TransformFunc
    72	        UnsafeDisableDeepCopy bool
    73	        EnableWatchBookmarks  bool
    74	        WatchErrorHandler     cache.WatchErrorHandlerWithContext
    75	}
    76	
    77	// NewInformers creates a new InformersMap that can create informers under the hood.
    78	func NewInformers(config *rest.Config, options *InformersOpts) *Informers {
    79	        newInformer := cache.NewSharedIndexInformer
    80	        if options.NewInformer != nil {
    81	                newInformer = options.NewInformer
    82	        }
    83	        return &Informers{
    84	                config:     config,
    85	                httpClient: options.HTTPClient,
    86	                scheme:     options.Scheme,
    87	                mapper:     options.Mapper,
    88	                tracker: tracker{
    89	                        Structured:   make(map[schema.GroupVersionKind]*Cache),
    90	                        Unstructured: make(map[schema.GroupVersionKind]*Cache),
    91	                        Metadata:     make(map[schema.GroupVersionKind]*Cache),
    92	                },
    93	                codecs:                serializer.NewCodecFactory(options.Scheme),
    94	                paramCodec:            runtime.NewParameterCodec(options.Scheme),
    95	                resync:                options.ResyncPeriod,
    96	                startWait:             make(chan struct{}),
    97	                namespace:             options.Namespace,
    98	                selector:              options.Selector,
    99	                transform:             options.Transform,
   100	                unsafeDisableDeepCopy: options.UnsafeDisableDeepCopy,
   101	                enableWatchBookmarks:  options.EnableWatchBookmarks,
   102	                newInformer:           newInformer,
   103	                watchErrorHandler:     options.WatchErrorHandler,
   104	        }
   105	}

}

   101	// objectTypeForListObject tries to find the runtime.Object and associated GVK
   102	// for a single object corresponding to the passed-in list type. We need them
   103	// because they are used as cache map key.
   104	func (ic *informerCache) objectTypeForListObject(list client.ObjectList) (*schema.GroupVersionKind, runtime.Object, error) {
   105	        gvk, err := apiutil.GVKForObject(list, ic.scheme)
   106	        if err != nil {
   107	                return nil, nil, err
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        // We need the non-list GVK, so chop off the "List" from the end of the kind.
   111	        gvk.Kind = strings.TrimSuffix(gvk.Kind, "List")
   112	
   113	        // Handle unstructured.UnstructuredList.
   114	        if _, isUnstructured := list.(runtime.Unstructured); isUnstructured {
   115	                u := &unstructured.Unstructured{}
   116	                u.SetGroupVersionKind(gvk)
   117	                return &gvk, u, nil

   131	        }

// GVKForObject finds the GroupVersionKind associated with the given object, if there is only a single such GVK.
func GVKForObject(obj runtime.Object, scheme *runtime.Scheme) (schema.GroupVersionKind, error) {
	// TODO(directxman12): do we want to generalize this to arbitrary container types?
	// I think we'd need a generalized form of scheme or something.  It's a
	// shame there's not a reliable "GetGVK" interface that works by default
	// for unpopulated static types and populated "dynamic" types
	// (unstructured, partial, etc)

	// check for PartialObjectMetadata, which is analogous to unstructured, but isn't handled by ObjectKinds
	_, isPartial := obj.(*metav1.PartialObjectMetadata)
	_, isPartialList := obj.(*metav1.PartialObjectMetadataList)
	if isPartial || isPartialList {
		// we require that the GVK be populated in order to recognize the object
		gvk := obj.GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind()
		if len(gvk.Kind) == 0 {
			return schema.GroupVersionKind{}, runtime.NewMissingKindErr("unstructured object has no kind")
		}
		if len(gvk.Version) == 0 {
			return schema.GroupVersionKind{}, runtime.NewMissingVersionErr("unstructured object has no version")
		}
		return gvk, nil
	}

// NewSharedInformer creates a new instance for the ListerWatcher. See NewSharedIndexInformerWithOptions for full details.
func NewSharedInformer(lw ListerWatcher, exampleObject runtime.Object, defaultEventHandlerResyncPeriod time.Duration) SharedInformer {
	return NewSharedIndexInformer(lw, exampleObject, defaultEventHandlerResyncPeriod, Indexers{})
}

// NewSharedIndexInformer creates a new instance for the ListerWatcher and specified Indexers. See
// NewSharedIndexInformerWithOptions for full details.
func NewSharedIndexInformer(lw ListerWatcher, exampleObject runtime.Object, defaultEventHandlerResyncPeriod time.Duration, indexers Indexers) SharedIndexInformer {
	return NewSharedIndexInformerWithOptions(
		lw,
		exampleObject,
		SharedIndexInformerOptions{
			ResyncPeriod: defaultEventHandlerResyncPeriod,
			Indexers:     indexers,
		},
	)
}

// NewSharedIndexInformerWithOptions creates a new instance for the ListerWatcher.
// The created informer will not do resyncs if options.ResyncPeriod is zero.  Otherwise: for each
// handler that with a non-zero requested resync period, whether added
// before or after the informer starts, the nominal resync period is
// the requested resync period rounded up to a multiple of the
// informer's resync checking period.  Such an informer's resync
// checking period is established when the informer starts running,
// and is the maximum of (a) the minimum of the resync periods
// requested before the informer starts and the
// options.ResyncPeriod given here and (b) the constant
// `minimumResyncPeriod` defined in this file.
func NewSharedIndexInformerWithOptions(lw ListerWatcher, exampleObject runtime.Object, options SharedIndexInformerOptions) SharedIndexInformer {
	realClock := &clock.RealClock{}

	processor := &sharedProcessor{clock: realClock}
	processor.listenersRCond = sync.NewCond(processor.listenersLock.RLocker())

	return &sharedIndexInformer{
		indexer:                         NewIndexer(DeletionHandlingMetaNamespaceKeyFunc, options.Indexers, WithStoreMetrics(options.Identifier, options.InformerMetricsProvider)),
		processor:                       processor,
		synced:                          make(chan struct{}),
		listerWatcher:                   lw,
		objectType:                      exampleObject,
		objectDescription:               options.ObjectDescription,
		resyncCheckPeriod:               options.ResyncPeriod,
		defaultEventHandlerResyncPeriod: options.ResyncPeriod,
		clock:                           realClock,
		cacheMutationDetector:           NewCacheMutationDetector(fmt.Sprintf("%T", exampleObject)),

    24	var logKind = logf.RuntimeLog.WithName("source").WithName("Kind")
    25	
    26	// Kind is used to provide a source of events originating inside the cluster from Watches (e.g. Pod Create).
    27	type Kind[object client.Object, request comparable] struct {
    28	        // Type is the type of object to watch.  e.g. &v1.Pod{}
    29	        Type object
    30	
    31	        // Cache used to watch APIs
    32	        Cache cache.Cache
    33	
    34	        Handler handler.TypedEventHandler[object, request]
    35	
    36	        Predicates []predicate.TypedPredicate[object]
    37	
    38	        // startedErr may contain an error if one was encountered during startup. If its closed and does not
    39	        // contain an error, startup and syncing finished.
    40	        startedErr  chan error
    41	        startCancel func()
    42	}
    43	
    44	// Start is internal and should be called only by the Controller to register an EventHandler with the Informer
    45	// to enqueue reconcile.Requests.
    46	func (ks *Kind[object, request]) Start(ctx context.Context, queue workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[request]) error {
    47	        if isNil(ks.Type) {
    48	                return fmt.Errorf("must create Kind with a non-nil object")
    49	        }
    50	        if isNil(ks.Cache) {
    51	                return fmt.Errorf("must create Kind with a non-nil cache")
    52	        }
    53	        if isNil(ks.Handler) {
    54	                return errors.New("must create Kind with non-nil handler")
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        // cache.GetInformer will block until its context is cancelled if the cache was already started and it can not
    58	        // sync that informer (most commonly due to RBAC issues).
    59	        ctx, ks.startCancel = context.WithCancel(ctx)
    60	        ks.startedErr = make(chan error, 1) // Buffer chan to not leak goroutines if WaitForSync isn't called
    61	        go func() {
    62	                var (
    63	                        i       cache.Informer
    64	                        lastErr error
    65	                )
    66	
    67	                // Tries to get an informer until it returns true,
    68	                // an error or the specified context is cancelled or expired.
    69	                if err := wait.PollUntilContextCancel(ctx, 10*time.Second, true, func(ctx context.Context) (bool, error) {
    70	                        // Lookup the Informer from the Cache and add an EventHandler which populates the Queue
    71	                        i, lastErr = ks.Cache.GetInformer(ctx, ks.Type)
    72	                        if lastErr != nil {
    73	                                kindMatchErr := &meta.NoKindMatchError{}
    74	                                switch {
    75	                                case errors.As(lastErr, &kindMatchErr):
    76	                                        logKind.Error(lastErr, "if kind is a CRD, it should be installed before calling Start",
    77	                                                "kind", kindMatchErr.GroupKind)
    78	                                case runtime.IsNotRegisteredError(lastErr):
    79	                                        logKind.Error(lastErr, "kind must be registered to the Scheme")
    80	                                default:
    81	                                        logKind.Error(lastErr, "failed to get informer from cache")
    82	                                }
    83	                                return false, nil // Retry.
    84	                        }
    85	                        return true, nil
    86	                }); err != nil {
    87	                        if lastErr != nil {
    88	                                ks.startedErr <- fmt.Errorf("failed to get informer from cache: %w", lastErr)
    89	                                return
    90	                        }
    91	                        ks.startedErr <- err
    92	                        return
    93	                }
    94	
    95	                handlerRegistration, err := i.AddEventHandlerWithOptions(NewEventHandler(ctx, queue, ks.Handler, ks.Predicates), toolscache.HandlerOptions{
    96	                        Logger: &logKind,
    97	                })
    98	                if err != nil {
    99	                        ks.startedErr <- err
   100	                        return
   101	                }
   102	                // First, wait for the cache to sync. For real caches this waits for startup.
   103	                // For fakes with Synced=false, this returns immediately allowing fast failure.
   104	                if !ks.Cache.WaitForCacheSync(ctx) {
   105	                        ks.startedErr <- errors.New("cache did not sync")
   106	                        close(ks.startedErr)
   107	                        return
   108	                }
   109	                // Then wait for this specific handler to receive all initial events.
   110	                if !toolscache.WaitForCacheSync(ctx.Done(), handlerRegistration.HasSynced) {
   111	                        ks.startedErr <- errors.New("handler did not sync")
   112	                }
   113	                close(ks.startedErr)
   114	        }()
   115	
   116	        return nil
   117	}
   118	
   119	func (ks *Kind[object, request]) String() string {
   120	        if !isNil(ks.Type) {
   121	                return fmt.Sprintf("kind source: %s", kindDescription(ks.Type))
   122	        }
   123	        return "kind source: unknown type"
   124	}
   125	
   126	func kindDescription(obj client.Object) string {
   127	        if _, ok := obj.(*metav1.PartialObjectMetadata); ok {
   128	                if gvk := obj.GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind(); !gvk.Empty() {
   129	                        return gvk.String()
   130	                }
   131	        }
   132	        return fmt.Sprintf("%T", obj)
   133	}
   134	
   135	// WaitForSync implements SyncingSource to allow controllers to wait with starting
   136	// workers until the cache is synced.
   137	func (ks *Kind[object, request]) WaitForSync(ctx context.Context) error {
   138	        select {
   139	        case err := <-ks.startedErr:
   140	                return err
   141	        case <-ctx.Done():
   142	                ks.startCancel()
   143	                if errors.Is(ctx.Err(), context.Canceled) {
   144	                        return nil
   145	                }
   146	                return fmt.Errorf("timed out waiting for cache to be synced for Kind %s", kindDescription(ks.Type))
   147	        }
   148	}
   149

   152	                v.Kind() == reflect.Interface ||
   153	                v.Kind() == reflect.Slice ||
   154	                v.Kind() == reflect.Map ||
   155	                v.Kind() == reflect.Chan ||

    78	func NewInformers(config *rest.Config, options *InformersOpts) *Informers {
    79	        newInformer := newSharedIndexInformer
    80	        if options.NewInformer != nil {
    81	                newInformer = options.NewInformer
    82	        }
    83	        return &Informers{

    86	                scheme:     options.Scheme,
    87	                mapper:     options.Mapper,
    88	                tracker: tracker{

    90	                        Unstructured: make(map[schema.GroupVersionKind]*Cache),
    91	                        Metadata:     make(map[schema.GroupVersionKind]*Cache),

   104	        }

   115	func objectDescription(obj runtime.Object) string {
   116	        switch obj.(type) {
   117	        case *metav1.PartialObjectMetadata, *metav1.PartialObjectMetadataList:
   118	                if gvk := obj.GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind(); !gvk.Empty() {
   119	                        return gvk.String()
   120	                }
   121	        }
   122	        return ""
   123	}

func objectDescription(obj runtime.Object) string {
	switch obj.(type) {
	case *metav1.PartialObjectMetadata, *metav1.PartialObjectMetadataList:
		if gvk := obj.GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind(); !gvk.Empty() {
			return gvk.String()
		}
	}
	return ""
}

	if description := objectDescription(obj); description != "" {
		return description
	}
	return fmt.Sprintf("%T", obj)

// Start starts the informer managed by a MapEntry.
// Blocks until the informer stops. The informer can be stopped
// either individually (via the entry's stop channel) or globally
// via the provided stop argument.
func (c *Cache) Start(stop <-chan struct{}) {
	// Stop on either the whole map stopping or just this informer being removed.
	internalStop, cancel := syncs.MergeChans(stop, c.stop)
	defer cancel()
	// Convert the stop channel to a context and then add the logger.
	c.Informer.RunWithContext(logr.NewContext(wait.ContextForChannel(internalStop), log))
}

   235	// Watch implements controller.Controller.
   236	func (c *Controller[request]) Watch(src source.TypedSource[request]) error {
   237	        c.mu.Lock()
   238	        defer c.mu.Unlock()
   239	
   240	        // Sources weren't started yet, store the watches locally and return.
   241	        // These sources are going to be held until either Warmup() or Start(...) is called.
   242	        if !c.startedEventSourcesAndQueue {
   243	                c.startWatches = append(c.startWatches, src)
   244	                return nil
   245	        }
   246	
   247	        c.LogConstructor(nil).Info("Starting EventSource", "source", src)
   248	        return src.Start(c.ctx, c.Queue)
   249	}

   253	        if c.LeaderElected == nil {
   254	                return true
   255	        }
   256	        return *c.LeaderElected

   259	// Warmup implements the manager.WarmupRunnable interface.
   260	func (c *Controller[request]) Warmup(ctx context.Context) error {
   261	        if c.EnableWarmup == nil || !*c.EnableWarmup {
   262	                return nil
   263	        }
   264	
   265	        c.mu.Lock()
   266	        defer c.mu.Unlock()
   267	
   268	        // Set the ctx so later calls to watch use this internal context
   269	        c.ctx = ctx
   270	
   271	        return c.startEventSourcesAndQueueLocked(ctx)
   272	}

   274	// Start implements controller.Controller.
   275	func (c *Controller[request]) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
   276	        // use an IIFE to get proper lock handling
   277	        // but lock outside to get proper handling of the queue shutdown
   278	        c.mu.Lock()
   279	        if c.Started {
   280	                return errors.New("controller was started more than once. This is likely to be caused by being added to a manager multiple times")
   281	        }
   282	
   283	        c.initMetrics()
   284	
   285	        // Set the internal context.
   286	        c.ctx = ctx
   287	
   288	        wg := &sync.WaitGroup{}
   289	        err := func() error {
   290	                defer c.mu.Unlock()
   291	
   292	                // TODO(pwittrock): Reconsider HandleCrash
   293	                defer utilruntime.HandleCrashWithLogger(c.LogConstructor(nil))
   294	
   295	                // NB(directxman12): launch the sources *before* trying to wait for the
   296	                // caches to sync so that they have a chance to register their intended
   297	                // caches.
   298	                if err := c.startEventSourcesAndQueueLocked(ctx); err != nil {
   299	                        return err
   300	                }
   301	
   302	                c.LogConstructor(nil).Info("Starting Controller")
   303	
   304	                // Launch workers to process resources
   305	                c.LogConstructor(nil).Info("Starting workers", "worker count", c.MaxConcurrentReconciles)
   306	                wg.Add(c.MaxConcurrentReconciles)
   307	                for i := 0; i < c.MaxConcurrentReconciles; i++ {
   308	                        go func() {
   309	                                defer wg.Done()
   310	                                // Run a worker thread that just dequeues items, processes them, and marks them done.
   311	                                // It enforces that the reconcileHandler is never invoked concurrently with the same object.
   312	                                for c.processNextWorkItem(ctx) {
   313	                                }
   314	                        }()
   315	                }
   316	
   317	                c.Started = true
   318	                return nil
   319	        }()
   320	        if err != nil {
   321	                return err
   322	        }
   323	
   324	        <-ctx.Done()
   325	        c.LogConstructor(nil).Info("Shutdown signal received, waiting for all workers to finish")
   326	        wg.Wait()
   327	        c.LogConstructor(nil).Info("All workers finished")
   328	        return nil
   329	}

   331	// startEventSourcesAndQueueLocked launches all the sources registered with this controller and waits
   332	// for them to sync. It returns an error if any of the sources fail to start or sync.
   333	func (c *Controller[request]) startEventSourcesAndQueueLocked(ctx context.Context) error {
   334	        var retErr error
   335	
   336	        c.didStartEventSourcesOnce.Do(func() {
   337	                queue := c.NewQueue(c.Name, c.RateLimiter)
   338	                if priorityQueue, isPriorityQueue := queue.(priorityqueue.PriorityQueue[request]); isPriorityQueue {
   339	                        c.Queue = priorityQueue
   340	                } else {
   341	                        c.Queue = &priorityQueueWrapper[request]{TypedRateLimitingInterface: queue}
   342	                }
   343	                go func() {
   344	                        <-ctx.Done()
   345	                        c.Queue.ShutDown()
   346	                }()
   347	
   348	                errGroup := &errgroup.Group{}
   349	                for _, watch := range c.startWatches {
   350	                        log := c.LogConstructor(nil)
   351	                        _, ok := watch.(interface {
   352	                                String() string
   353	                        })
   354	                        if !ok {
   355	                                log = log.WithValues("source", fmt.Sprintf("%T", watch))
   356	                        } else {
   357	                                log = log.WithValues("source", fmt.Sprintf("%s", watch))

   360	                        errGroup.Go(func() error {
   361	                                // Use a timeout for starting and syncing the source to avoid silently
   362	                                // blocking startup indefinitely if it doesn't come up.
   363	                                sourceStartCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, c.CacheSyncTimeout)

+func objectDescription(obj runtime.Object) string {
+	switch obj.(type) {
+	case *metav1.PartialObjectMetadata, *metav1.PartialObjectMetadataList:
+		if gvk := obj.GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind(); !gvk.Empty() {
+			return gvk.String()
+		}
+	}
+	return ""
+}

+		return description
+	}

+}

+func newSharedIndexInformer(lw cache.ListerWatcher, exampleObject runtime.Object, defaultEventHandlerResyncPeriod time.Duration, indexers cache.Indexers) cache.SharedIndexInformer {
+	return cache.NewSharedIndexInformerWithOptions(lw, exampleObject, cache.SharedIndexInformerOptions{
+		ResyncPeriod:      defaultEventHandlerResyncPeriod,
+		Indexers:          indexers,
+		ObjectDescription: objectDescription(exampleObject),
+	})
+}
+
+func objectDescription(obj runtime.Object) string {
+	switch obj.(type) {
+	case *metav1.PartialObjectMetadata, *metav1.PartialObjectMetadataList:
+		if gvk := obj.GetObjectKind().GroupVersionKind(); !gvk.Empty() {
+			return gvk.String()
+		}
+	}
+	return ""
+}
+
+func informerTypeDescription(obj runtime.Object) string {
+	if description := objectDescription(obj); description != "" {
+		return description
+	}
+	return fmt.Sprintf("%T", obj)
+}
+
